  • demand_heatmap.html
  • flight_ranking.html
  • train_productivity.html
  • connection_quality.html

  • Passenger Coverage: 43.6% (1,340/3,070 passengers)
  • Flight Coverage: 11/24 flights (45.8%)
  • Total Synchronizations: 15
  • Average connections per covered flight: 1.4
